				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2 style="text-align: center;"><strong><span style="color: #ffffff;">Alissa’s Style:</span></strong></h2></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_2">
				
				
				
				
				<a href="https://storybehindthecloth.com/alissas-style/"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="1080" height="1028" src="https://storybehindthecloth.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Alissas-Story-A-Style-Journey-Blog-Posts-Outfits-Adventures-Thoughts-About-Life-e1588050847259.png" alt="Alissas Story A Style Journey Blog Posts Outfits Adventures Thoughts About Life e1588050847259" title="Home 12" srcset="https://storybehindthecloth.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Alissas-Story-A-Style-Journey-Blog-Posts-Outfits-Adventures-Thoughts-About-Life-e1588050847259.png 1080w, https://storybehindthecloth.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Alissas-Story-A-Style-Journey-Blog-Posts-Outfits-Adventures-Thoughts-About-Life-980x980.png 980w, https://storybehindthecloth.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/Alissas-Story-A-Style-Journey-Blog-Posts-Outfits-Adventures-Thoughts-About-Life-480x480.png 480w" sizes="auto, (min-width: 0px) and (max-width: 480px) 480px, (min-width: 481px) and (max-width: 980px) 980px, (min-width: 981px) 1080px, 100vw" class="wp-image-5641"></span></a>
			</div><div class="et_pb_button_module_wrapper et_pb_button_2_wrapper et_pb_button_alignment_center et_pb_module ">
				<a class="et_pb_button et_pb_button_2 et_pb_bg_layout_light" href="https://storybehindthecloth.com/alissas-style/" data-icon="">Browse Alissa's Style</a>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_4 et_pb_with_background et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_2">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_4  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_code et_pb_code_0">
				
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_4  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><span style="color: #ffffff;">Behind the clothes we wear are countless stories of who we are, who we’ve been, and who we want to be.</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffffff;"></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffffff;">Style is an art; a deep form of expression that may often be difficult to put to words, but is meaningful and full of feeling.</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffffff;"></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffffff;">Behind our choice of fabric, color, texture, and fit are memories, emotions, and ideals that we share in code.</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffffff;"></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffffff;">Whether consciously or subconsciously, we’re remembering things about ourselves and sharing it with the world through our outfits.</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffffff;"></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffffff;">It’s not always pretty either–sometimes our clothes have something to say about fear, pain, and insecurity–But what good, beautiful story doesn’t include these things, anyway?</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffffff;"></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffffff;">Fashion is a unique form of exploration, and personal style gives so much opportunity for self-discovery.</span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffffff;"></span></p>
<p><span style="color: #ffffff;">Join me on this adventure of </span><span style="color: #ffffff;">unveiling what is meaningful behind fashion, and learning to authentically share our true selves through style.</span></p>
<p> </p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_3">
